Hello world. This is Morocco â€” not the glossy postcards you see, but the hidden truth. Families who lost everything in the 2023 earthquake are still living in tents, waiting for homes that never come. Hospitals are overcrowded and without medicine, mothers wait for hours only to be told there is nothing for their children.
